##############################
#   Post-Apocalypse Events   #
##############################

add_namespace = RAD			# International
add_namespace = RAD_RUS		# Russia
add_namespace = RAD_EU		# Europe
add_namespace = RAD_NA		# North America
add_namespace = RAD_SA		# South America
add_namespace = RAD_EA		# East Asia
add_namespace = RAD_CH		# China
add_namespace = RAD_IN		# India
add_namespace = RAD_SEA		# South East Asia
add_namespace = RAD_AF		# Africa
add_namespace = RAD_ME		# Middle East
add_namespace = RAD_DBG		# Debug

#############
#   DEBUG   #
#############

country_event = {
	id = RAD_DBG.0
	title = "Debug"
	desc = "Removes all demilitarized zones and buildings once anarchy has taken over fully, which takes 16 in-game days, even though you can't tell due to the overlay."
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RAD_DBG.0" }

	option = {
		name = "RAD_DBG.0 Firing"
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_demilitarized_zone = yes }
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = RAD_DBG.1
	title = "Debug"
	desc = "Tells the PostApoc_events_begin scripted effect to do its job"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RAD_DBG.1" }

	option = {
		name = "RAD_DBG.1 Firing"
		PostApoc_events_begin = yes
	}
}

##############
#   RUSSIA   #
##############

country_event = {
	id = RAD_RUS.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RAD_RUS.1" }
	title = RAD_RUS.1.t
	desc = RAD_RUS.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_post_apoc_radio

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = TNO_my_world_is_on_fire_how_about_yours
	}

	option = {
		name = RAD_RUS.1.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				33 = {
					country_event = { id = RAD_RUS.9 days = 15 }
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { has_global_flag = OMS_PostApoc_Event }
					}
				}
				33 = {
					country_event = { id = RAD_RUS.18 days = 15 }
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { has_global_flag = WRW2_PostApoc_Event }
					}
				}
				34 = {
					country_event = { id = RAD_RUS.22 days = 15 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event RAD_RUS.23" }
	title = RAD_RUS.23.t
	desc = RAD_RUS.23.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_post_apoc_classical

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = TNO_my_world_is_on_fire_how_about_yours
	}

	option = {
		name = RAD_RUS.23.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				33 = {
					country_event = { id = RAD_RUS.7 days = 15 }
				}
				33 = {
					country_event = { id = RAD_RUS.13 days = 15 }
				}
				34 = {
					country_event = { id = RAD_RUS.28 days = 15 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
